### Maintnance

#Clears all the jobs a character has
rtp_flush_jobs = {
	hidden_tooltip = {
		remove_title = server_mt
		remove_title = guard_mt
		remove_title = barterer_mt
		remove_title = beggar_mt
		remove_title = postulant_mt

		remove_title = minstrel_mt
		remove_title = veteran_mt
		remove_title = shop_assistant_mt
		remove_title = pickpocket_mt
		remove_title = preacher_mt

		remove_title = town_crier_mt
		remove_title = bailif_mt
		remove_title = peddler_mt
		remove_title = poacher_mt
		remove_title = scribe_mt

		remove_title = diplomat_mt
		remove_title = officer_mt
		remove_title = shop_keeper_mt
		remove_title = brigand_mt
		remove_title = librarian_mt

		remove_title = sellsword_mt
		remove_title = holy_warrior_mt
		remove_title = bandit_mt
	}
}

#Clears all the buildings a landless character has
rtp_flush_buildings = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_owns_house #I own a house
		}
		wealth = 25
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_owns_chickens #I own chickens
		}
		wealth = 50
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_owns_statuette #I own a statuette
		}
		wealth = 75
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_owns_fence #I own a fence
		}
		wealth = 100
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_owns_cows #I own cow
		}
		wealth = 125
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_owns_tub #I own a tub
		}
		wealth = 150
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_owns_candles #I own some candles
		}
		wealth = 175
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_owns_fireplace #I own a fireplace
		}
		wealth = 200
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_owns_sheep #I own sheep
		}
		wealth = 225
	}

	clr_global_flag = rtp_owns_estate #I own an estate lvl 1

#Removes corruption of the realm
rtp_remove_corruption_se = {
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption20_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption19_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption18_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption17_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption16_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption15_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption14_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption13_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption12_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption11_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption10_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption9_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption8_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption7_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption6_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption5_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption4_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption3_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_corruption1_em
}

#Cancels the appropriate plot
rtp_cancel_plot_st = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_plot = plot_gain_title
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_gain_title
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_plot = plot_gain_vassal_title
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_gain_vassal_title
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_kill_character
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_kill_spouse
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_seize_trade_post
	}
}

#Assigns appropriate tooltip for the prices of the artifacts
rtp_assign_price_tooltip_st = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 1
		}
		ROOT = {
			show_scope_change = no
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "rtp_lvl1_price_ct"
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 2
		}
		ROOT = {
			show_scope_change = no
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "rtp_lvl2_price_ct"
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 3
		}
		ROOT = {
			show_scope_change = no
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "rtp_lvl3_price_ct"
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 4
		}
		ROOT = {
			show_scope_change = no
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "rtp_lvl4_price_ct"
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 5
		}
		ROOT = {
			show_scope_change = no
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "rtp_lvl5_price_ct"
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 6
		}
		ROOT = {
			show_scope_change = no
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = "rtp_lvl0_price_ct"
			}
		}
	}
}

#Assigns the cost for the first artifact
rtp_assign_artifact_cost1_se = {
	new_artifact = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				quality == 1
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 2
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				quality == 2
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				quality == 3
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 6
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				quality == 4
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 8
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				quality == 5
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 10
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				quality == 6
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ROOT = {
		random_list = {
			2 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.1
				}
			}
			4 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.2
				}
			}
			8 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			16 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.4
				}
			}
			32 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			64 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.6
				}
			}
			128 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.7
				}
			}
			256 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.8
				}
			}
			512 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.9
				}
			}
			1024 = {
			}
			512 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.1
				}
			}
			256 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.2
				}
			}
			128 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.3
				}
			}
			64 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.4
				}
			}
			32 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			16 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			8 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.7
				}
			}
			4 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.8
				}
			}
			2 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.9
				}
			}
			1 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Assigns the selling price for the the artifact
rtp_assign_sellprice_artifact_cost_se = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 1
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_variable = {
				which = rtp_artifact_cost
				value = 2
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 2
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_variable = {
				which = rtp_artifact_cost
				value = 4
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 3
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_variable = {
				which = rtp_artifact_cost
				value = 6
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 4
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_variable = {
				which = rtp_artifact_cost
				value = 8
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 5
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_variable = {
				which = rtp_artifact_cost
				value = 10
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			quality == 6
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_variable = {
				which = rtp_artifact_cost
				value = 20
			}
		}
	}

	ROOT = {
		random_list = {
			2 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.1
				}
			}
			4 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.2
				}
			}
			8 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.3
				}
			}
			16 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.4
				}
			}
			32 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
			64 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.6
				}
			}
			128 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.7
				}
			}
			256 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.8
				}
			}
			512 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 0.9
				}
			}
			1024 = {
			}
			512 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.1
				}
			}
			256 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.2
				}
			}
			128 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.3
				}
			}
			64 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.4
				}
			}
			32 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.5
				}
			}
			16 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.6
				}
			}
			8 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.7
				}
			}
			4 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.8
				}
			}
			2 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 1.9
				}
			}
			1 = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = rtp_artifact_cost
					value = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gives rewards associated with a major conflict
rtp_give_major_conflict_rewards_se = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = rtp_invasion_prestige #Do it for prestige
		}
		prestige = 50
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = rtp_invasion_gold #Do it for gold
		}
		wealth = 50
	}
	else = {
		character_event = {
			id = RTPlandless.27 #Invasion Barony/Land
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

#Give a big amount of gold
rtp_give_big_gold_se = {
	random_list = {
		10 = {
			wealth = 20
		}
		15 = {
			wealth = 15
		}
		25 = {
			wealth = 10
		}
		50 = {
			wealth = 5
		}
	}
}

#Give a big amount of society currency
rtp_give_big_currency_se = {
	random_list = {
		10 = {
			change_society_currency = 25
		}
		15 = {
			change_society_currency = 20
		}
		25 = {
			change_society_currency = 15
		}
		50 = {
			change_society_currency = 10
		}
	}
}

#Fills the society ranks with new characters
rtp_create_society_members_se = {
	#Martial
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = rtp_chalcedonian #Chalcedonian game
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = rtp_chalcedonian #Chalcedonian game
					has_global_flag = rtp_schism #The schism happens
				}
			}
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_society_rank_full = {
						society = rtp_martial_catholic
						rank = 1
					}
				}
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = catholic
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = cathar
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = fraticelli
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = waldensian
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = lollard
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
				}
				new_character = {
					join_society = rtp_martial_catholic
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								society = {
									any_society_member = {
										is_society_grandmaster = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						set_society_grandmaster = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = rtp_chalcedonian #Chalcedonian game
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = rtp_chalcedonian #Chalcedonian game
					has_global_flag = rtp_schism #The schism happens
				}
			}
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_society_rank_full = {
						society = rtp_martial_orthodox
						rank = 1
					}
				}
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = orthodox
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = bogomilist
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = monothelite
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = iconoclast
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = paulician
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
				}
				new_character = {
					join_society = rtp_martial_orthodox
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								society = {
									any_society_member = {
										is_society_grandmaster = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						set_society_grandmaster = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rtp_chalcedonian #Chalcedonian game
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = rtp_schism #The schism happens
			}
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_society_rank_full = {
						society = rtp_martial_chalcedonian
						rank = 1
					}
				}
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				random_list = {
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = chalcedonian
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
					10 = {
						create_character = {
							age = 20
							random_traits = yes
							female = no
							religion = iconoclast
							culture = THIS
							dynasty = none
						}
					}
				}
				new_character = {
					join_society = rtp_martial_chalcedonian
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								society = {

	#Diplomacy

		limit = {

				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = rtp_chalcedonian #Chalcedonian game
				}

### Troops

#Gives potential volunteers to the holding
rtp_assign_volunteers_se = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			num_of_max_settlements == 1
		}
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers
					value = 5
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
					value = -5
				}
			}
			20 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers
					value = 10
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
					value = -10
				}
			}
			20 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers
					value = 15
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
					value = -15
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			num_of_max_settlements == 2
		}
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers
					value = 10
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
					value = -10
				}
			}
			20 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers
					value = 15
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
					value = -15
				}
			}
			20 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers
					value = 20
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
					value = -20
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			num_of_max_settlements == 3
		}
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers
					value = 15
				}
				change_variable = {

	else_if = {

				change_variable = {

			}
			20 = {
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers
					value = 45
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
					value = -45
				}
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			location = {
				culture = ROOT
				religion = ROOT
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
			value = 0.1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			location = {
				OR = {
					culture = ROOT
					religion = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
			value = 0.2
		}
	}
	else = {
		multiply_variable = {
			which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
			value = 0.3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					rtp_is_mercenary = yes
					rtp_is_holy_order = yes
				}
			}
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = global_rtp_potential_volunteers_cost
			value = 0.2
		}
	}
}

#Raise potential volunteers - Landless

		spawn_unit = {
			province = location
			home = location
			owner = ROOT
			leader = ROOT
			troops = {
				light_infantry = { 750 750 }
				archers = { 300 300 }
				heavy_infantry = { 250 250 }
				light_cavalry = { 200 200 }
				pikemen = { 150 150 }
				knights = { 100 100 }
			}
			earmark = rtp_mercenaries
			disband_on_peace = yes
			reinforces = yes
			reinforce_rate_multiplier = 0.1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_character_flag = rtp_payx8
		}
		spawn_unit = {
			province = location
			home = location
			owner = ROOT
			leader = ROOT
			troops = {
				light_infantry = { 750 750 }
				archers = { 350 350 }
				heavy_infantry = { 300 300 }
				light_cavalry = { 250 250 }
				pikemen = { 200 200 }
				knights = { 150 150 }
			}
			earmark = rtp_mercenaries
			disband_on_peace = yes
			reinforces = yes
			reinforce_rate_multiplier = 0.1
		}
	}
}

#Gives random troops to Mercenaries/Holy Orders
rtp_give_troops_se = {
	random_list = {
		25 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = rtp_troops
				value = 25
			}
		}
		25 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = rtp_troops
				value = 50
			}
		}
		25 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = rtp_troops
				value = 75
			}
		}
		25 = {
			change_variable = {
				which = rtp_troops
				value = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

### Naval

#Assigns outcome chances for naval combat - Attacker
rtp_assign_naval_outcome1_se = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial = 20
		}
		set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial < 20
			martial = 18
		}
		random = {
			chance = 95
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial < 18
			martial = 16
		}
		random = {
			chance = 90
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial < 16
			martial = 14
		}
		random = {
			chance = 85
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial < 14
			martial = 12
		}
		random = {
			chance = 80
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial < 12
			martial = 10
		}
		random = {
			chance = 75
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial < 10
			martial = 8
		}
		random = {
			chance = 70
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial < 8
			martial = 6
		}
		random = {
			chance = 65
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial < 6
			martial = 4
		}
		random = {
			chance = 60
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			martial > event_target:rtp_defending_admiral
			martial < 4
		}
		random = {
			chance = 55
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
	else = {
		random = {
			chance = 50
			set_character_flag = rtp_naval_victor
		}
	}
}

#Outcome of the naval combat - Attacker
rtp_naval_outcome1_se = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				trait = rtp_admiral_tr
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 50

			add_trait = rtp_admiral_tr
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			can_have_more_leadership_traits = yes
			NOT = {
				trait = rtp_naval_expert_tr
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 25

			add_trait = rtp_naval_expert_tr
		}
	}
	
	event_target:rtp_defending_admiral = {
		show_scope_change = no
		save_event_target_as = rtp_defending_admiral #The defending admiral
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					trait = rtp_admiral_tr
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50

				add_trait = rtp_admiral_tr
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				can_have_more_leadership_traits = yes
				NOT = {
					trait = rtp_naval_expert_tr
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25

				add_trait = rtp_naval_expert_tr
			}
		}
	}

	any_character = {
		show_scope_change = no
		limit = {
			at_location = PREV
			NOT = {
				same_realm = PREV
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			75 = {

			}
			20 = {
				imprison = event_target:rtp_attacking_liege
			}
			5 ={
				death = {
					death_reason = death_accident_drowning
				}
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				government = rtp_privateer_g
				trait = viking
				trait = pirate
				trait = ravager
				trait = sea_queen
				trait = seaking
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				wealth = 20
				event_target:rtp_defending_liege = {
					show_scope_change = no
					wealth = -20
				}
			}
			20 = {
				wealth = 15
				event_target:rtp_defending_liege = {
					show_scope_change = no
					wealth = -15
				}
			}
			20 = {
				wealth = 10
				event_target:rtp_defending_liege = {
					show_scope_change = no
					wealth = -10
				}
			}
			20 = {
				wealth = 5
				event_target:rtp_defending_liege = {
					show_scope_change = no
					wealth = -5
				}
			}
			20 = {}
		}
	}
}

### Siege

#Assigns casualties to the attackers
rtp_siege_casualties_se = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			TECH_FORTIFICATIONS_CONSTRUCTION = 8
		}
		ROOT = {
			siege = {
				enemy = {
					troops = -0.16
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			TECH_FORTIFICATIONS_CONSTRUCTION = 7
		}
		ROOT = {
			siege = {
				enemy = {
					troops = -0.14
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			TECH_FORTIFICATIONS_CONSTRUCTION = 6
		}
		ROOT = {
			siege = {
				enemy = {
					troops = -0.12
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			TECH_FORTIFICATIONS_CONSTRUCTION = 5
		}
		ROOT = {
			siege = {
				enemy = {
					troops = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			TECH_FORTIFICATIONS_CONSTRUCTION = 4
		}
		ROOT = {
			siege = {
				enemy = {
					troops = -0.08
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			TECH_FORTIFICATIONS_CONSTRUCTION = 3
		}
		ROOT = {
			siege = {
				enemy = {
					troops = -0.06
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			TECH_FORTIFICATIONS_CONSTRUCTION = 2
		}
		ROOT = {
			siege = {
				enemy = {
					troops = -0.04
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			TECH_FORTIFICATIONS_CONSTRUCTION = 1
		}
		ROOT = {
			siege = {
				enemy = {
					troops = -0.02
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Trait Points

#Gives the appropriate Holy Warrior Trait for the religion
rtp_give_holy_warrior_trait_se = {
	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = religion_group
		christian = 			{ add_trait = crusader }
		muslim = 				{ add_trait = mujahid }
		zoroastrian_group = 	{ add_trait = gondi_shahansha }
		jewish_group = 			{ add_trait = shaddai }
		indian_group = 			{ add_trait = rtp_maharathi_tr }
	}

	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = religion
		norse_pagan = 						{ add_trait = valhalla_bound }
		norse_pagan_reformed = 				{ add_trait = valhalla_bound }
		aztec = 							{ add_trait = eagle_warrior }
		aztec_reformed = 					{ add_trait = eagle_warrior }
		zun_pagan = 						{ add_trait = sun_warrior }
		zun_pagan_reformed = 				{ add_trait = sun_warrior }
		finnish_pagan = 					{ add_trait = ukkos_shield }
		finnish_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = ukkos_shield }
		west_african_pagan = 				{ add_trait = nyames_shield }
		west_african_pagan_reformed = 		{ add_trait = nyames_shield }
		slavic_pagan = 						{ add_trait = peruns_chosen }
		slavic_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = peruns_chosen }
		baltic_pagan = 						{ add_trait = romuvas_own }
		baltic_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = romuvas_own }
		hellenic_pagan = 					{ add_trait = ares_own }
		hellenic_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = ares_own }
		tengri_pagan = 						{ add_trait = tengri_warrior }
		tengri_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = tengri_warrior }
		bon = 								{ add_trait = kailash_guardian }
		bon_reformed = 						{ add_trait = kailash_guardian }
	}
}

#Gives the appropriate Martial Society Trait for the religion

	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = religion_group
		christian = 			{ add_trait = christian_leader }

		zoroastrian_group = 	{ add_trait = zoroastrian_leader }
		jewish_group = 			{ add_trait = jewish_leader }
		indian_group = 			{ add_trait = eastern_leader }
	}

	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = religion
		norse_pagan = 						{ add_trait = norse_leader }
		norse_pagan_reformed = 				{ add_trait = norse_leader }
		aztec = 							{ add_trait = aztec_leader }
		aztec_reformed = 					{ add_trait = aztec_leader }
		zun_pagan = 						{ add_trait = zun_leader }
		zun_pagan_reformed = 				{ add_trait = zun_leader }
		finnish_pagan = 					{ add_trait = finnish_leader }
		finnish_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = finnish_leader }
		west_african_pagan = 				{ add_trait = west_african_leader }
		west_african_pagan_reformed = 		{ add_trait = west_african_leader }
		slavic_pagan = 						{ add_trait = slavic_leader }
		slavic_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = slavic_leader }
		baltic_pagan = 						{ add_trait = baltic_leader }
		baltic_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = baltic_leader }
		hellenic_pagan = 					{ add_trait = hellenic_leader }
		hellenic_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = hellenic_leader }

		tengri_pagan_reformed = 			{ add_trait = tengri_leader }

		bon_reformed = 						{ add_trait = bon_leader }
	}
}

#Gives adventurer points
rtp_give_adventurer_points_se = {
	hidden_tooltip = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = rtp_veteran_warrior
					value = 1
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = rtp_veteran_warrior
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				which = rtp_veteran_warrior
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				trait = adventurer
			}
			check_variable = {
				which = rtp_veteran_warrior
				value = 5
			}
		}
		add_trait = adventurer
	}
}

#Gives holy warrior points
rtp_give_holy_warrior_points_se = {
	hidden_tooltip = {
		liege = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_war = {
						using_cb = religious
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							check_variable = {
								which = rtp_holy_warrior
								value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						change_variable = {
							which = rtp_holy_warrior
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					ROOT = {
						set_variable = {
							which = rtp_holy_warrior
							value = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			rtp_has_holy_warrior_trait_st = no
			check_variable = {
				which = rtp_holy_warrior
				value = 2
			}
		}
		rtp_give_holy_warrior_trait_se = yes
	}
}

#Gives gladiator points
rtp_give_gladiator_points_se = {
	hidden_tooltip = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = rtp_gladiator
					value = 1
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = rtp_gladiator
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				which = rtp_gladiator
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				trait = gladiator
			}
			check_variable = {
				which = rtp_gladiator
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_trait = gladiator
	}
}

### Laws

#Assigns laws
rtp_assign_laws_se = {
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_slavery_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_slavery_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_trade_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_trade_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_resettlement_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_resettlement_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_welfare_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_welfare_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_production_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_production_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_property_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_property_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_banking_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_banking_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_holidays_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_holidays_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_role_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_role_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_consecrated_grounds_0_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_consecrated_grounds_2_em
	remove_character_modifier = rtp_membership_0_em

#Gives the penalty for being overstretched
rtp_assign_overstretched_modifier_se = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOR = {
				trait = adventurer
				has_character_flag = is_charlemagne
				has_character_flag = is_child_of_destiny
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					realm_size = 240
				}
				AND = {
					tier = KING
					realm_size = 190
				}
				AND = {
					tier = DUKE
					realm_size = 140
				}
				AND = {
					tier = COUNT
					realm_size = 90
				}
			}
			capital_scope = {
				TECH_LEGALISM = 8
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = EMPEROR
			}
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = realm_size
				345 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption20_em years = 2 } }
				340 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption19_em years = 2 } }
				325 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption18_em years = 2 } }

	else_if = {
		limit = {

				trait = adventurer

		if = {

			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = realm_size
				295 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption20_em years = 2 } }

				255 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption12_em years = 2 } }
				250 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption11_em years = 2 } }
				245 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption10_em years = 2 } }
				240 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption9_em years = 2 } }
				235 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption8_em years = 2 } }
				230 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption7_em years = 2 } }
				225 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption6_em years = 2 } }
				220 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption5_em years = 2 } }
				215 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption4_em years = 2 } }
				210 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption3_em years = 2 } }

				175 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption6_em years = 2 } }
				170 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption5_em years = 2 } }
				165 = { rtp_remove_corruption_se = yes add_character_modifier = { modifier = rtp_corruption4_em years = 2 } }

	}

	}
}

#Assigns laws associated with barons
rtp_assign_baron_laws = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			rtp_is_republic = yes
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			gender_succ = agnatic
			add_law = {
				law = rtp_republic_election_succ
				cooldown = no
				opinion_effect = no
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			rtp_is_theocracy = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = catholic
					religion = fraticelli
				}
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = succ_catholic_bishopric
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = rtp_theocracy_election_succ
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				rtp_is_mercenary = yes
				rtp_is_holy_order = yes
			}
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			gender_succ = agnatic
			add_law = {
				law = rtp_mercenary_election_succ
				cooldown = no
				opinion_effect = no
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_tribal = yes
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			gender_succ = agnatic
			add_law = {
				law = succ_elective_gavelkind
				cooldown = no
				opinion_effect = no
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_feudal = yes
			religion_group = muslim
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			gender_succ = agnatic
			add_law = {
				law = succ_turkish_succession
				cooldown = no
				opinion_effect = no
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		any_demesne_title = {
			gender_succ = agnatic
			add_law = {
				law = succ_gavelkind
				cooldown = no
				opinion_effect = no
			}
		}
	}
}

#Assigns laws associated with counts and above
rtp_assign_count_laws = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				holding_type = castle
				holding_type = tribal
			}
			ROOT = {
				rtp_is_mercenary = yes
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_government_type = rtp_mercenary_g
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = rtp_mercenary_election_succ
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			holding_type = castle
			ROOT = {
				rtp_is_holy_order = yes
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_government_type = order_government
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = rtp_mercenary_election_succ
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			holding_type = city
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_government_type = rtp_republic_g
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = rtp_republic_election_succ
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			holding_type = temple
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					religion = catholic
					religion = fraticelli
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_government_type = rtp_theocracy_g
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = succ_catholic_bishopric
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			holding_type = temple
			ROOT = {
				NOR = {
					religion = catholic
					religion = fraticelli
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_government_type = rtp_theocracy_g
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = rtp_theocracy_election_succ
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			holding_type = tribal
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_government_type = tribal_government
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = succ_elective_gavelkind
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				holding_type = castle
				holding_type = temple
			}
			ROOT = {
				culture_group = tibetan_group
				OR = {
					religion = bon
					religion = bon_reformed
					religion = buddhist
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_government_type = theocratic_feudal_government
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = succ_gavelkind
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				holding_type = castle
				holding_type = temple
			}
			ROOT = {
				religion_group = muslim
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			set_government_type = muslim_government
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = succ_turkish_succession
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		ROOT = {
			set_government_type = feudal_government
			any_demesne_title = {
				gender_succ = agnatic
				add_law = {
					law = succ_gavelkind
					cooldown = no
					opinion_effect = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gives opinion penalty for decreasing council powers
rtp_assign_decreased_council_power_se = {
	holder_scope = {
		any_vassal = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_decreased_council_power
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_decreased_council_power
				years = 5
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_decreased_council_power
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_decreased_council_power
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

#Gives opinion bonuses for increasing council powers
rtp_assign_increased_council_power_se = {
	holder_scope = {
		any_vassal = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_increased_council_power
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_increased_council_power
				years = 5
			}
		}
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_increased_council_power
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_increased_council_power
				years = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

### Duels

#Evaluates score for weapon vs armor
rtp_evaluate_weapon_vs_armor_se = {
	#Me
	if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				has_artifact_flag = cleaver #Good vs Cloth
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = cloth
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				OR = {
					has_artifact_flag = sword #Good vs Light
					has_artifact_flag = throwing #Good vs Light
				}
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = light
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				OR = {
					has_artifact_flag = polearm #Good vs Medium
					has_artifact_flag = axe #Good vs Medium
					has_artifact_flag = bow #Good vs Medium
				}
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = medium
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				OR = {
					has_artifact_flag = spear #Good vs Heavy
					has_artifact_flag = mace #Good vs Heavy
					has_artifact_flag = flail #Good vs Heavy
				}
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = heavy
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				OR = {
					has_artifact_flag = dagger #Good vs Plate
					has_artifact_flag = crossbow #Good vs Plate
					has_artifact_flag = hammer #Good vs Plate
				}
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = plate
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 1
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 2
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 3
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 4
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 5
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 5
		}
	}

	#You
	if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				has_artifact_flag = cleaver #Good vs Cloth
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = cloth
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				OR = {
					has_artifact_flag = sword #Good vs Light
					has_artifact_flag = throwing #Good vs Light
				}
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = light
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				OR = {
					has_artifact_flag = polearm #Good vs Medium
					has_artifact_flag = axe #Good vs Medium
					has_artifact_flag = bow #Good vs Medium
				}
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = medium
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				OR = {
					has_artifact_flag = spear #Good vs Heavy
					has_artifact_flag = mace #Good vs Heavy
					has_artifact_flag = flail #Good vs Heavy
				}
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = heavy
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				OR = {
					has_artifact_flag = dagger #Good vs Plate
					has_artifact_flag = crossbow #Good vs Plate
					has_artifact_flag = hammer #Good vs Plate
				}
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = plate
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 1
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 2
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 3
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 4
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_armor = {
				has_artifact_flag = shield
				quality == 5
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 5
		}
	}
}

#Evaluates score for weapon vs weapon
rtp_evaluate_weapon_vs_weapon_se = {
	#Me
	if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 1
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 2
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 1
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 3
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 1
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 4
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 1
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 5
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 2
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 3
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 2
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 4
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 2
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 5
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 3
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 4
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 3
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 5
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 4
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 5
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}

	#You
	if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 1
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 2
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 1
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 3
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 1
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 4
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 1
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 5
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 2
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 3
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {

				quality == 2

				quality == 4

		}

			value = 2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 2
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 5
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 3
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 4
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = duel_result_score
			value = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			event_target:rtp_combatant2_weapon = {
				quality == 3
			}
			event_target:rtp_combatant1_weapon = {
				quality == 5
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {

	else_if = {
